{"kind": "blogger#postList", "nextPageToken": "CgkIChig4L_J4CUQy4Ca9ZL8nrwx", "items": [{"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "706460616069549306", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-02-12T23:27:00+05:30", "updated": "2012-05-10T21:07:27+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzM2NjY0MjQ3NTg1Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/02/port-royal-pirate-haven-capt-ajit.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/706460616069549306", "title": "PORT ROYAL, THE PIRATE HAVEN --  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-SQ-z_YOKZig/TVbHgC2q01I/AAAAAAAADaQ/XNIMPuL0Lpg/s1600/P.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"151\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-SQ-z_YOKZig/TVbHgC2q01I/AAAAAAAADaQ/XNIMPuL0Lpg/s320/P.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-30SxP8pSRPg/TVbHkKANimI/AAAAAAAADaU/cNv8pm3aAbE/s1600/images+%252814%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-30SxP8pSRPg/TVbHkKANimI/AAAAAAAADaU/cNv8pm3aAbE/s1600/images+%252814%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">In 1992, my chemical tanker was anchored at Kingston bay. I was in my cabin, talking to the agent on VHF. Suddenly the whole ship lurched, and i felt that my ship had been rammed by some other ship. So i ran on the bridge wings , and found nothing special. The sea was calm with no ripples or wake.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">I noticed my entire crew and officers were already standing on the poop deck. I was the only Indian, in command, &nbsp;the rest were Jamaican, with a Russian Chief Engineer thrown in for good measure..&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The crew shouted , to me that Kingston just had a earth quake. The shore buildings were very near, and i could see people running out of all buildings. In the distance I could see dust from a hill landslide.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">That reminded me of Port Royal. Port Royal was the richest city in the world , till&nbsp;at 11:43 a.m. on June 7, 1692, a severe earth quake measuring 7.5 on the Richter scale, decimated everything. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-U9AYxIOgYgI/TVbHp7-GSxI/AAAAAAAADaY/goHhxiGvor4/s1600/a.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"201\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-U9AYxIOgYgI/TVbHp7-GSxI/AAAAAAAADaY/goHhxiGvor4/s320/a.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-fPt_fdO-ZpE/TVbHtjYlyBI/AAAAAAAADac/-qqwp8X0Ass/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-fPt_fdO-ZpE/TVbHtjYlyBI/AAAAAAAADac/-qqwp8X0Ass/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Out of 4 forts, only one Fort Charles remained standing. Everything else slid under the sea in two minutes, killing 3000 people.. Before the earthquake, the town consisted of 6,500 inhabitants living in about 2,000 brick and wood &nbsp;buildings. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qHgjXDahGew/TVbI9L5wazI/AAAAAAAADbg/OPKfgr1Z5zc/s1600/images+%252818%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qHgjXDahGew/TVbI9L5wazI/AAAAAAAADbg/OPKfgr1Z5zc/s1600/images+%252818%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cgGeTcLodWI/TVbH2luTFUI/AAAAAAAADak/2DeMEYVHhvg/s1600/220px-Pirate_Flag_of_Rack_Rackham.svg.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-cgGeTcLodWI/TVbH2luTFUI/AAAAAAAADak/2DeMEYVHhvg/s1600/220px-Pirate_Flag_of_Rack_Rackham.svg.png\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Indeed it could be said, that this horrific event was God\u2019s punishment for unlawful proceedings ( void in human consciousness ) by a group of sinful people. It was home to some of the vilest individuals on earth, and had tonnes of stolen gold. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-JCNLSKQN9WQ/TVbH7Wy52PI/AAAAAAAADao/ul972UlnvSc/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-JCNLSKQN9WQ/TVbH7Wy52PI/AAAAAAAADao/ul972UlnvSc/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">On the very night of the quake, those who survived the disaster in the destroyed town were said to have been back at their \"old trade of drinking, swearing and whoring\". No preacher who ever entered the port hoping to convert the wayward masses of the island ever lasted more than a few weeks before departing to more civilized places.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-JCNLSKQN9WQ/TVbH7Wy52PI/AAAAAAAADao/ul972UlnvSc/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-JCNLSKQN9WQ/TVbH7Wy52PI/AAAAAAAADao/ul972UlnvSc/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-zsyR8zCXMAg/TVbIAEIKmJI/AAAAAAAADas/l8CVRoI2Qv0/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-zsyR8zCXMAg/TVbIAEIKmJI/AAAAAAAADas/l8CVRoI2Qv0/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">From 1660 to 1692, Port Royal therefore became a haven for rogues such as the Welshman, Henry Morgan and 'three-fingered' Jack Rack ham.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uS6lHbRjvkQ/TVbIF3SzzaI/AAAAAAAADa0/uvBy-QCo8lo/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uS6lHbRjvkQ/TVbIF3SzzaI/AAAAAAAADa0/uvBy-QCo8lo/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">After this 1692 disaster, Port Royal's commercial role was steadily taken over by the new City of Kingston.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-h_4KofJ8dzg/TVbILOASFaI/AAAAAAAADa4/uGx_0z1aSbo/s1600/images+%252824%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-h_4KofJ8dzg/TVbILOASFaI/AAAAAAAADa4/uGx_0z1aSbo/s1600/images+%252824%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Port Royal is the inspiration for movies like Pirates of the Caribbean.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-x0fGd2gdNYg/TVbIOdLih4I/AAAAAAAADa8/CH2g1U26HaU/s1600/images+%252813%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-x0fGd2gdNYg/TVbIOdLih4I/AAAAAAAADa8/CH2g1U26HaU/s1600/images+%252813%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"></span>Spain maintained control over the island of Jamaica for 146 years, until the English invasion of 1655. Port Royal provided a safe harbour initially for privateers and subsequently for pirates plying the shipping lanes to and from Spain and Panama. Buccaneers found Port Royal appealing for several reasons.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-EyuekiQL75c/TVbJDQm2TFI/AAAAAAAADbk/SJxbFQK34A4/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-EyuekiQL75c/TVbJDQm2TFI/AAAAAAAADbk/SJxbFQK34A4/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Its proximity to trade routes allowed them easy access to prey Spanish ships sailing back from South America with gold. When they returned to their sanctuary, no mortal dared enter Port Royal in pursuit, as it was guarded by 4 forts. This pirate haven was one of the best defended ports in the world and most feared.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\">By the 1660s, the city had gained a reputation as the Sodom of the New World where most residents were pirates, cut throats, or prostitutes. . During a twenty-year period that ended in 1692, nearly 8000 people lived in Port Royal.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0BtsyOLICiE/TVbJz5JWzJI/AAAAAAAADbo/pBPGU9GJRrY/s1600/images+%252825%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0BtsyOLICiE/TVbJz5JWzJI/AAAAAAAADbo/pBPGU9GJRrY/s1600/images+%252825%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\">The colonial city of Port Royal, the largest English-held city in the Caribbean, was a haven for pirates and other less-than-savory characters under British rule, Buccaneers, gamblers, prostitutes etc. In 1687, when Port Royal was commonly referred to as \u201cthe wickedest city on earth. The harbour was large enough to accommodate several ships and provided a place to careen and repair these vessels.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oyq6_55KjiI/TVbIS9bz8mI/AAAAAAAADbA/T5m1Oq8GPJg/s1600/T.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oyq6_55KjiI/TVbIS9bz8mI/AAAAAAAADbA/T5m1Oq8GPJg/s320/T.jpg\" width=\"296\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\">This was the place where pirates from all over the world, spend their shore leave. Port Royal transformed into a criminal nest. Here all pirates were equal. There were hundreds of brothels and taverns. At the height of its popularity, the city had one drinking house for every ten residents . They drank bombo or bumboo, a mixture of rum, water, sugar, and nutmeg.&nbsp; Rum fustian was another popular drink that blended raw eggs with sugar, sherry, gin, and beer.&nbsp; Pirates also enjoyed beer, sherry, brandy, and port. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-q6RTPLQi_XA/TVbIWrvHYwI/AAAAAAAADbE/xUz2JTiqyk4/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-q6RTPLQi_XA/TVbIWrvHYwI/AAAAAAAADbE/xUz2JTiqyk4/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\">They played cards or rolled dice, although most articles of agreement forbade gambling on board ships to prevent arguments that divided the crew or proved fatal to one or more participants. When ashore, pirates squandered their booty on drink, women, and games of chance.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-efFLdWm7KkI/TVbIctv7xvI/AAAAAAAADbI/1gbRXKy0iM4/s1600/N.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"253\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-efFLdWm7KkI/TVbIctv7xvI/AAAAAAAADbI/1gbRXKy0iM4/s320/N.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\">Pirates or Port Royal emulated gentleman merchants by wearing knee breeches, stockings, embroidered waistcoats, lace-trimmed shirts, long coats, and shoes with silver buckles and high heels, to impress the ladies.&nbsp; And some of these ladies were indeed rich and pretty. A few wore powdered wigs or ornate jewelry.&nbsp; They acquired these brightly colored garments as shares of booty taken from captured ships.&nbsp; While at sea, they usually wore one outfit until the garments were no better than rags.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-2bsLh_B1PkE/TVbIzV-vIFI/AAAAAAAADbc/Itc1bApbbUg/s1600/images+%252817%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-2bsLh_B1PkE/TVbIzV-vIFI/AAAAAAAADbc/Itc1bApbbUg/s1600/images+%252817%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\">Most of these Pirates were desperadoes. Many of the men were killed and their families were shipped off to the dungeons of the Inquisition; those men that survived turned to a life of piracy.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-7fIkprerXCY/TVbIfWAfskI/AAAAAAAADbM/eqDuhx7-NFY/s1600/download+%25281%2529.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-7fIkprerXCY/TVbIfWAfskI/AAAAAAAADbM/eqDuhx7-NFY/s1600/download+%25281%2529.JPG\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\">Have you heard the song \"Sixteen men on a dead man's ship? Yo ho ho and a bottle of rum\"? That jingle told the tale of 16 pirates marooned on the BVI's island of Dead Chest with a single bottle of grog. The fight which ensued left no survivors. Such was the brutality of the pirates.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-M_hdW7rtKRc/TVbIpOitBLI/AAAAAAAADbU/tdhK8Ky6WKU/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; line-height: 150%;\">When I took my wife and children to Disney land in USA and Japan, it was indeed amusing to the dummy Pirates serenading the ladies, drinking , swearing and generally living it up like a \u201c sailor on shore leave\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; API gravity is measured by a hydrometer instrument having a scale graduated in degrees API.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Backhaul</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A deviation to move cargo on the return leg of a voyage for the purpose of minimizing ballast mileage and thereby reducing transportation cost. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Bare Boat Charter </span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">- A Charter in which the bare ship is chartered without crew; the charterer, for a stipulated sum taking over the vessel with a minimum of restrictions usually for 10 or more years. See Demise Charter. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Barrel</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The standard unit of liquid volume in the petroleum industry. It is equal to 42 U.S. gallons. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Canceling Date</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A stated date after which, if a vessel is not ready to load, the intending charterers have the option of canceling the charter. The passing of the canceling date leaves the owner\u2019s obligation unimpaired unless the charterer releases him. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Contract of Affreightment (COA)</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A service contract under which a ship owner agrees to transport a specified quantity of fuel products or specialty products, at a specified rate per ton between designated loading and discharge ports. This type contract differs from a spot or consecutive voyage charter in that no particular vessel is specified. (Rates are usually discounted below other forms of contracts.) <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Spot (Voyage) Charter</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A charter for a particular vessel to move a single cargo between specified loading port(s) and discharge port(s) in the immediate future. Contract rate (spot rate) covers total operating expenses such as port charges, bunkering, crew expenses, insurance, repairs, and canal tolls. style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; tab-stops: 138.0pt; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Classification of Petroleum</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - Classes \"A-C\" of petroleum are considered flammable and have a flash point of 80\u00b0 F or below. Examples of these classes range from very light napthas (Class A) to most crude oils (Class C). Class D cargoes such as kerosene and heavy crudes are considered combustible and have a flash point above 80\u00b0 F but below 150\u00b0 F. Class E cargoes are the heavier fuel oils and lubricating oils and have a flash point above 150\u00b0 F. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Clean Service</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - Tanker transportation of products lighter than residual fuels, e.g. distillates, including No. 2 Heating Oil. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Closed Gauging System</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A method of obtaining measurements of the tank contents without opening the tank. This may be accomplished by using automatic tank gauges or by taking measurements through a pressure/vapor lock standpipe. This type of gauging is done extensively on vessels with inert gas systems. Such a system that allows no vapors to be lost to the atmosphere is a true closed system while other types that allow minimum vapors to be lost to the atmosphere are called \"restricted systems.\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Dispatch</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The function of issuing voyage instructions or sa</span></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 13px;\">iling orders to vessels. Also an agreed amount to be charged by terminals for prompt vessel turn around.</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 13px;\"><br />\n</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Displacement Tonnage</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - Expressed in tons it is the weight the water displaced by the vessel which in turn is the weight of the vessel at that time. The vessel\u2019s light displacement is the weight of the vessel only and the vessel\u2019s loaded displacement is the weight of the vessel and all cargo, stores, fuel, water, etc. on board. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Disponent Owner</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - Charterer who has sublet the vessel and is acting as the owner per the terms of the contract. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Ensign</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The flag carried by a ship as insignia of her nationality. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Filling Density</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The ratio of the weight of liquid in a tank to the weight of distilled water at 60\u00b0 F. the tank will hold. It is expressed as a percent. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Flame Screen</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> (or Arrester) - A device comprised of a fine wire gauze that is fitted into the discharge end of a vent line. It prevents the passage of flame, but will allow vapor to pass through. Flame screens are also fitted to removable ullage plugs used to cover ullage holes on cargo tank tops. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Force Majeure</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - Clause permitting contract to be broken in the event of uncontrollable events, e.g. war, strike government action, which preclude its fulfillment. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Free Discharge (FD)</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The charterer is responsible for the cost of unloading the cargo. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Free In And Out (FIO)</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The charterer is responsible for both the costs of loading and unloading the cargo. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Free on Board (FOB)</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The charterer is responsible for the cost of loading the cargo. </span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt; letter-spacing: 0.1pt;\">I</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt;\">n<span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.15pt;\"> </span>a<span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.1pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Gas Free Certificate</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A certificate issued by a chemist after sampling the air in a tanker's cargo tanks after the cargo has been pumped out. It is endorsed with one of the following notations: (1) Safe for men, (2) Not safe for fire, (3) Safe for men and fire, (4) Not safe. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">General Average</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A general contribution of money paid by all parties concerned in a marine adventure in direct proportion to their several interests when a voluntary or deliberate sacrifice has been made of one or more of the party\u2019s goods in time of peril with a view to saving the remainder of the property. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Gross Tonnage</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The internal capacity of a vessel measured in units of 100 cubic feet.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Guarantee Items</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - Repair of guarantee items that develop during the first year of service of a new vessel and are usually corrected by the builder under a guarantee. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">In Class</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> \u2013 A vessel currently meeting all the requirements of its Classification Society is \"in-class\". -0.15pt;\">e</span></span><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.15pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Inert Gas (IG)</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A gas used by marine tank vessels to displace air in cargo tanks to reduce oxygen content to 8 percent or less by volume and thus reduce possibility of fire or explosion. The inert gas used is usually nitrogen, carbon dioxide or a mixture of gases such as flue gas.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Inert Gas System (IGS)</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A mechanical method of introducing inert gas into a vessel\u2019s tanks. An inert gas is one which has little or no ability to react with other gases, or to heat. Examples of inert gases are nitrogen and CO2. Shipboard inert gas systems utilize CO2, either from flue gas sources or from inert gas generators. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Inerting</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A procedure used to reduce the oxygen content of a vessel\u2019s cargo spaces to 8 percent or less by volume by introducing an \"inert\" gas blanket such as nitrogen or carbon dioxide or a mixture of gases such as flue gas.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt; letter-spacing: -0.1pt;\">Inh</span></b><b><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt; letter-spacing: 0.1pt;\">i</span></b><b><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt; letter-spacing: -0.1pt;\">b</span></b><b><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt; letter-spacing: 0.1pt;\">i</span></b><b><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt;\">t<span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.25pt;\">o</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.1pt;\">r</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.1pt;\">s</span>:<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.25pt;\"> </span></span></b><span style=\"color: 0.1pt;\">iz</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.15pt;\">a</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.1pt;\">t</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.05pt;\">i</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.25pt;\">o</span>n</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 13px;\"><br />\n</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Innage</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The amount of space within a tank that is occupied by oil. Innages are sometimes called soundings or body gauges. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Independent Inspector (Cargo Surveyor)</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A person or organization of persons acting independently, but on behalf of, one or more parties involved in the transfer, storage, inventory or analysis of a commodity for purposes of determining the quantity, and/or quality of a commodity. They may also be assigned to the calibration of various measurement instruments and/or storage tanks ashore or on vessels.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Intake Certificate</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A document issued by the shipper indicating the amount of cargo loaded aboard the vessel as calculated from the shore tank gauges. Freight is paid on the basis of these figures. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Intertanko</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> \u2013 International association of independent tanker owners. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Isherwood System</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A method framing a vessel which employs closely spaced longitudinals with extra heavy floors spaced further apart. Most tankers use this type of framing system. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Jettison</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The act of pumping cargo/ chemicals &nbsp;overboard to lighten/ prevent explosion in an emergency. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 1.7pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Lay days</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The period of time described in the charter party during which the owner must tender his ship for loading. The charterer is not obliged to start loading before the commencement of lay days. The charterer may cancel the charter if the ship does not tender prior to the expiration of lay days. style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Letter of Protest or Notice of Apparent Discrepancy</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - A letter issued by any participant in a custody transfer citing any condition with which issue is taken. This serves as a written record that the particular action or finding was questioned at the time of occurrence.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Lighter</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - <b>1)</b> General name for a broad, flat-bottomed boat used in transporting cargo between a vessel and the shore. The distinction between a lighter and a barge is more in the manner of use than in equipment. The term \"lighter\" refers to a short haul, generally in connection with loading and unloading operations of vessels in harbor while the term \"barge\" is more often used when the cargo is being carried to its destination or over a long distance. <b>2)</b> To load or discharge cargo to or from another vessel. VTBL vessel to be lightered. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Lighterage</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - <b>1)</b> Fee charged for conveying cargo by lighters or barges. <b>2)</b> Area where vessels normally lighter. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\">Lightering</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - Conveying cargo with another vessel known as a lighter from a ship to shore, or voyage. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - The law that permits a shipowner to restrict his liability to the value of this vessel after the accident plus the earnings for the voyage. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"><br Holes</span></b><span style=\"font-size: 10pt;\"> - Holes in the bottoms of stringers through which cargo flows through to the suction strums. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div style=\"text-align: 0.65pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.1pt;\">i</span>n<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.9pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.15pt;\">t</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.15pt;\">a</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.25pt;\">r</span>d<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.65pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.25pt;\">vo</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.25pt;\">e</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.15pt;\">e</span>n<span style=\"letter-spacing: 1pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.1pt;\">t</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.25pt;\">B</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt; letter-spacing: 0.1pt;\">il</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 10pt;\">l<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.3pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.25pt;\">o</span>f<span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.1pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.15pt;\">L</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.1pt;\">a</span>d<span
