, &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-08msPGEwq1I/TVPFyDvT3hI/AAAAAAAADVI/7f1YUssPpTQ/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-08msPGEwq1I/TVPFyDvT3hI/AAAAAAAADVI/7f1YUssPpTQ/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">They were to have no part in the management of the business.Anyone who disputed this arrangement would lose their interest in the Estate.(The last stipulation was specifically designed to seal the mouths of anyone who might feel like breaking with the family. Rothschild obviously felt that there were a lot of things under the family<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">'rug'</span></em><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>that should never see the light of day).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The mighty strength of the House of Rothschild was based on a variety of important factors:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><strong><span style=\"font-weight: normal; line-height: 150%;\">(A)</span></strong><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Complete secrecy resulting from total family control of all business dealings;<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><strong><span style=\"font-weight: normal; line-height: 150%;\">(B)</span></strong><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">An uncanny, one could almost say a supernatural ability to see what lay ahead and to take full advantage of it. The whole family was driven by an insatiable lust for the accumulation of wealth and power, and<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><strong><span style=\"font-weight: normal; line-height: 150%;\">(C)</span></strong><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Total ruthlessness in all business dealings.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Biographer Frederic Morton, in The Rothschilds, tells us that Mayer Amschel Rothschild and his five sons were<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">\"wizards\"</span></em><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>of finance,and<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">\"fiendish calculators\"</span></em><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>who were motivated by a<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">\"demonic drive\"</span></em><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>to succeed in their secret undertakings.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8KAfRj5bqdU/TVPF9kfJ0WI/AAAAAAAADVQ/0_b_swxUjdU/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8KAfRj5bqdU/TVPF9kfJ0WI/AAAAAAAADVQ/0_b_swxUjdU/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">OK, now the Waterloo epsode in greater detail--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-d8FUdmU6L30/TVPF6b5_IrI/AAAAAAAADVM/RhqLRmxfHKI/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-d8FUdmU6L30/TVPF6b5_IrI/AAAAAAAADVM/RhqLRmxfHKI/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Upon the battle of Waterloo depended the future of the European continent.If the Grande Armee of Napoleon emerged victorious France would be undisputed master of all she surveyed on the European front. If Napoleon was crushed into submission England would hold the balance of power in Europe and would be in a position to greatly expand its sphere of influence.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Historian John Reeves, a Rothschild partisan, reveals in his book TheRothschilds, Financial Rulers of the Nations, 1887, page 167, that<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">\"one cause of his [Nathan's] success was the secrecy with which he shrouded,and the tortuous policy with which he misled those who watched him the keenest.\"</span></em><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-style: normal;\"><br />\n</span></em></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">There were vast fortunes to be made - and lost - on the outcome of the Battle of Waterloo. The Stock Exchange in London was at fever pitch as traders awaited news of the outcome of this battle of the giants. If Britain lost,English consuls would plummet to unprecedented depths. If Britain was victorious,the value of the consul would leap to dizzying new heights.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">As the two huge armies closed in for their battle to the death, Nathan Rothschild had his agents working feverishly on both sides of the line together the most accurate possible information as the battle proceeded. Additional Rothschild agents were on hand to carry the intelligence bulletins to a Rothschild command post strategically located nearby.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Late on the afternoon of June 15, 1815, a Rothschild representative jumped on board a specially chartered boat and headed out into the channel in a hurried dash for the English coast. In his possession was a top secret report from Rothschild's secret service agents on the progress of the crucial battle.This intelligence data would prove indispensable to Nathan in making some vital decisions.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The special agent was met at Folkstone the following morning at dawn by Nathan Rothschild himself. After quickly scanning the highlights of the report Rothschild was on his way again, speeding towards London and the Stock Exchange.<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Arriving at the Exchange amid frantic speculation on the outcome of the battle, Nathan took up his usual position beside the famous<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">'Rothschild Pillar.'</span></em><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp; </span>Without a sign of emotion, without the slightest change official expression the stony-faced, flint eyed chief of the House of Rothschild gave a predetermined signal to his agents who were stationed nearby.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Rothschild agents immediately began to dump consuls on the market. As hundred of thousands of dollars worth of consuls poured onto the market their value started to slide. Then they began to plummet.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Nathan continued to lean against<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">'his'</span></em><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>pillar, emotionless, expressionless. He continued to sell, and sell and sell. Consuls kept on falling. Word began to sweep through the Stock Exchange:<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">\"Rothschild knows.\" \"Rothschild knows.\" \"Wellington has lost at Waterloo.\" &nbsp;Nathan's carrier pigeon had already delivered the news that Napoleon had lost.</span></em><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-style: normal;\"><br />\n</span></em></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The selling turned into a panic as people rushed to unload their<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">'worthless' </span></em>consuls or paper money for gold and silver in the hope of retaining at least part of their wealth. Consuls continued their nosedive towards oblivion. After several hours of feverish trading the consul lay in ruins. It was selling for about five cents on the dollar.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Nathan Rothschild, emotionless as ever, still leaned against his pillar. He continued to give subtle signals. But these signals were different. They were so different that only the highly trained Rothschild agents could detect the change. On the cue from their boss, dozens of Rothschild agents made their way to the order desks around the Exchange and bought every consul in sight for just a<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">'song'!</span></em><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-style: normal;\"><br />\n</span></em></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">A short time later the<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">'official'</span></em><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>news arrived in the British capital. &nbsp;&nbsp;England was now the master of the European scene.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Within seconds the consul sky rocketed to above its original value. As the significance of the British victory began to sink into the public consciousness, the value of consuls rose even higher.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Napoleon had<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><em><span style=\"font-style: normal;\">'met his Waterloo.'</span></em><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp; </span>Nathan had bought control of the British economy. Overnight, his already vast fortune was multiplied twenty times over.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-sKdPIgA7JiU/TVYGeTybwmI/AAAAAAAADZk/iXDv7tqNW0Y/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-sKdPIgA7JiU/TVYGeTybwmI/AAAAAAAADZk/iXDv7tqNW0Y/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">Napoleons trusted Doctor had been bribed to lose the leeches which sucked the pus from his inflammed piles, the night before he lost Waterloo- and he could NOT ride his horse, and be in command at the seat of battle.</span> </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-tRkUjWm6fPU/TVP-9o77IYI/AAAAAAAADWc/rgzdTQ-W05A/s1600/images+%252826%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-tRkUjWm6fPU/TVP-9o77IYI/AAAAAAAADWc/rgzdTQ-W05A/s1600/images+%252826%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Following their crushing defeat at Waterloo, the French struggled to get back on their feet financially. In 1817 they negotiated a substantial loan from the prestigious French banking house of Ouvrard and from the well-known bankers Baring Brothers of London. &nbsp;The Rothschilds had been left on the outside looking in.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The following year the French government was in need of another loan.As the bonds issued in 1817 with the help of Ouvrard and Baring Brothers were increasing in value on the Paris market, and in other European financial centers, it appeared certain that the French government would retain the services of these two distinguished banking houses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The Rothschild brothers tried most of the gimmicks in their vast repertoire to influence the French government to give them the business. Their efforts were in vain.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OJeE77VrQj8/TVP_UzEuBXI/AAAAAAAADWg/4n3CYUW8gNU/s1600/images+%252827%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OJeE77VrQj8/TVP_UzEuBXI/AAAAAAAADWg/4n3CYUW8gNU/s1600/images+%252827%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The French aristocrats, who prided themselves on their elegance and superior breeding, viewed the Rothschilds as mere peasants, upstarts who needed to be kept in their place. The fact that the Rothschilds had vast financial resources, lived in the most luxurious homes and were attired in the most elegant and expensive clothes obtainable cut no ice with the highly class conscious French nobility. The Rothschilds were viewed as uncouth \u2013 lacking in social graces. If we are to believe most historical accounts, their appraisal of the first generation Rothschilds was probably valid.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">One major piece of armament in the Rothschild arsenal the French had overlooked or ignored - their unprecedented cunning in the use and manipulation of money.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">On November 5, 1818, something very unexpected occurred. After a year of steady appreciation the value of the French government bonds began to fall. With each passing day the decline in their value became more pronounced.Within a short space of time other government securities began to suffer too.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">The atmosphere in the court of Louis XVIII was tense. Grim faced aristocrats pondered the fate of the country. They hoped for the best but feared the worst! The only people around the French court who weren't deeply concerned were James and Karl Rothschild. They smiled - but said nothing!<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Slowly a sneaking suspicion began to take shape in the minds of some onlookers. Could those Rothschild brothers be the cause of the nation's economic woes? Could they have secretly manipulated the bond market and engineered the panic?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">They had! <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">During October 1818, Rothschild agents, using their masters' limitless reserves, had bought huge quantities of the French government bonds issued through their rivals Ouvrard and Baring Brothers. This caused the bonds to increase in value. It was distributed in the early 1920s by Henry Ford.<br /><br /><span style=\"color: red;\">https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_International_Jew</span><br /><br />The Dearborn Independent, also known as The Ford International Weekly, was a weekly newspaper established in 1901, and published by Henry Ford from 1919 through 1927. The paper reached a circulation of 900,000 by 1925, second only to the New York Daily News run from the shadows by Jew Rothschild.<br /><br />Henry Ford knew that Jew Rothschild would start world wars to carve out the state of Israel and to make money out of war. Ford wrote that parasite Jews, in their role as financiers, contributed nothing of value to society.<br /><br />Ford once bit into a candy bar and, finding it not as good as it once had been, said \"The Jews have taken hold of it. They've cheapened it to make more money\".<br /><br />In 1915 Ford blamed Jews for instigating World War I, saying \"I know who caused the war: German-Jewish bankers.\"<br /><br />In 1925, Ford said \"What I oppose most is the international Jewish money power that is met in every war. That is what I oppose \u2013 a power that has no country and that can order the young men of all countries out to death.\"<br /><br />One of the articles, \"Jewish Power and America's Money Famine\", asserted that the power exercised by Jews over the nation's supply of money was insidious, depriving farmers and others outside the banking coterie of money when they needed it most. The article asked the question: \"Where is the American gold supply? ... It may be in the United States but it does not belong to the United States.\" It concluded that Jews controlled the gold supply and, hence, American money<br />Another article, \"Jewish Idea Molded Federal Reserve System\", was a reflection of Ford's distrust of the Federal Reserve System and its proponent, Paul Warburg. Ford believed the Federal Reserve system was secretive and insidious<br /><br />Many issues of the Independent comment extensively upon The Protocols of the Elders of Zion. text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0yaaTJimEN0/TjY2wn-DUzI/AAAAAAAAE5U/VLVPrZsZem8/s1600/imagesCAAW8X3E.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0yaaTJimEN0/TjY2wn-DUzI/AAAAAAAAE5U/VLVPrZsZem8/s1600/imagesCAAW8X3E.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nWATERLOO , MARSHAL NEY AND THE ROTHSCHILD CONSPIRACY</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hJiRRqIP9FM/TjY2222EBvI/AAAAAAAAE5Y/JstlgTwsMD0/s1600/imagesCAYH8XS6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hJiRRqIP9FM/TjY2222EBvI/AAAAAAAAE5Y/JstlgTwsMD0/s1600/imagesCAYH8XS6.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nTwo decades ago while passing St Helena I took my ship close to the island ( 1300 miles west of Angola ) to see what it is like. It was a desolate mountain popping out of the sea.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE6chiP5hI/AAAAAAAAA9A/YMQltUxukgs/s1600/imagesCA4SNV2J.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE6chiP5hI/AAAAAAAAA9A/YMQltUxukgs/s1600/imagesCA4SNV2J.jpg\" style=\"cursor: move;\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nNapoleon spent 6 years here in exile till be was poisoned by arsenic. Arsenic preserved his body . Much later his shrivelled tiny penis with a single ball was put for auction which failed to secure the bottom reserve price. But this man had balls.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nNapoleon had sensitive olfactory senses. He got a perfume made for his wife Josephine. I had bought this for my wife--and she says it is the best in her collection.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nNapoleon who ruled France was born to Italian parents , who spoke Italian at home.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nThe original Mona Lisa ( without eyebrows ) used to hang in his bed room.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE7bhUHwWI/AAAAAAAAA9I/hNrU1KxMUsc/s1600/imagesCAY93VFG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE7bhUHwWI/AAAAAAAAA9I/hNrU1KxMUsc/s1600/imagesCAY93VFG.jpg\" style=\"cursor: move;\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nHe would NOT have lost the battle of Waterloo in 1815 -- but for his inability to be mobile. He could not ride a horse, due to acute inflammation of piles -- it would have been too painful. Napoleon once upon a time could sleep on horseback.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE7CPbQ0pI/AAAAAAAAA9E/M53GlJygxPU/s1600/imagesCA84U3W4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE7CPbQ0pI/AAAAAAAAA9E/M53GlJygxPU/s1600/imagesCA84U3W4.jpg\" style=\"cursor: move;\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nLord Wellington had once remarked that Napoleon's presence in the battle field was like having an extra 50000 troops. He did not have to make his troops scream HEIL SEIG --the famous magic rallying cry of Hitler.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TD4h5Y4iQOU/TjY2-14QTMI/AAAAAAAAE5c/xSEsHj4yOcE/s1600/imagesCAONW301.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TD4h5Y4iQOU/TjY2-14QTMI/AAAAAAAAE5c/xSEsHj4yOcE/s1600/imagesCAONW301.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nHe used leeches to suck out the abcess at the rectum. But on the night before his defeat , his doctor lost the leeches.<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">The&nbsp;fabulously rich opium drug runners Rothschild bribed the doctor to lose the leeches</span></span><span style=\"font-size: large;\">.</span>&nbsp;</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-edwwL8QYP04/TVYGJBAjnWI/AAAAAAAADZg/eX2eCPakO3U/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-edwwL8QYP04/TVYGJBAjnWI/AAAAAAAADZg/eX2eCPakO3U/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\">A fortune was made by the Rotchschild family on the battle of Waterloo. &nbsp;Forbes does NOT dare to say that Rothschild family is the richest in the world, a dozen times more than the current No 1 of 2011.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/--J5NMB6ZQmo/TjY3FM4t0xI/AAAAAAAAE5g/Mi2nCHGHB64/s1600/imagesCALIQYYZ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/--J5NMB6ZQmo/TjY3FM4t0xI/AAAAAAAAE5g/Mi2nCHGHB64/s1600/imagesCALIQYYZ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 22px;\"><em>Opium smugglers of British East India company, James and Nathan Rothschilds &nbsp;who came up with the Battle of Waterloo scheme.&nbsp;The brothers financed both sides of the famous battle at Waterloo, between the French and the English.&nbsp;With advanced knowledge of the British victory ( using a trained carrier pigeon ) , Nathan Rothschild spread lies that the British had been defeated, which caused a crash in the value of British Government bonds.&nbsp;</em></span></span></span><br />\n<em><br />\n</em><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><em><span style=\"line-height: 22px;\">While panicked English investors sold up their life savings, Nathan Rothschild bought-up their bonds for pennies on the dollar.&nbsp;When official news of the British victory at Waterloo arrived, the English bond-market skyrocketed and so did Nathan Rothschild's wealth.&nbsp;In one foul swoop, the Demon Brothers had double-crossed the English masses and taken control of the Bank of England.&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 22px;\">Flaunting their tremendous wealth, the brothers went on a lavish spending spree.&nbsp;By 1823 the Rothschilds were guardians of the entire papal treasure and took over the financial operations of the Catholic Church and the Pope.</span></em></span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<em><br />\n</em></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE7_bTM31I/AAAAAAAAA9Q/m6XQjW7SKRc/s1600/untitled.bmp\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><em><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE7_bTM31I/AAAAAAAAA9Q/m6XQjW7SKRc/s1600/untitled.bmp\" style=\"cursor: move;\" /></em></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nThere was no plan B -- so he was injected with a strong painkiller which made him mentally dull. His gout too was out of control due to stress.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nHis second in command Marshall Ney could not deliver the goods. He is said to have fought well and five horses were killed under him.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Fp7FOVLhutI/TjY3Lm3Ph-I/AAAAAAAAE5k/oFL1ccATquU/s1600/imagesCA5N4CUH.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Fp7FOVLhutI/TjY3Lm3Ph-I/AAAAAAAAE5k/oFL1ccATquU/s1600/imagesCA5N4CUH.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">There is another school of thought that Rothschild bribed Ney.&nbsp; Ney had a showdown with Napoleon, the first time he abdicated.&nbsp; Wehn Napoleon said \" The army will obey me !\", Ney had replied \" The army will obey its generals \" .&nbsp; It was well known that Ney was NOT Napoleons man. </span></em><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-HYl8sqx3JUk/TjY3ZlcumEI/AAAAAAAAE5o/ooh5ZP_4q-E/s1600/imagesCADKTRZ2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"150\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-HYl8sqx3JUk/TjY3ZlcumEI/AAAAAAAAE5o/ooh5ZP_4q-E/s320/imagesCADKTRZ2.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Ney was sent to Napoleon, just 3 days before the Battle of Waterloo in a mysterious manner. Ney did NOT obey Napoleons order sent to him at Frasnes to engage a retreating Wellington. Ney ordered d'Erlons corps to turn back from Ligny on June 16th depriving Napoleon of the chance to destroy Bluchers army.</span></em></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-F0z5JhDxhRA/TjY3iRjz3-I/AAAAAAAAE5s/0VT-5o0ObaQ/s1600/untitled.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-F0z5JhDxhRA/TjY3iRjz3-I/AAAAAAAAE5s/0VT-5o0ObaQ/s1600/untitled.png\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nNapoleon went inside the great pyramid and came out pale and frightened, as if he had a premonition of the future. Tomb robbers had a history and tradition of knocking off the noses of Egyptian sarcophagi to neutralise curses.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE8Xc4GetI/AAAAAAAAA9U/tKJahwoEYK0/s1600/imagesCA94WLIO.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE8Xc4GetI/AAAAAAAAA9U/tKJahwoEYK0/s1600/imagesCA94WLIO.jpg\" style=\"cursor: move;\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nThe local guides at the Pyramids in Egypt told me that megalomaniac Napoleon shot off the nose of the Sphinx with a cannon.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE7yBxl6VI/AAAAAAAAA9M/2BCNc1i_keI/s1600/imagesCA74WLNV.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE7yBxl6VI/AAAAAAAAA9M/2BCNc1i_keI/s1600/imagesCA74WLNV.jpg\" style=\"cursor: move;\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nIt is well known that this megalomaniac had once razed a fort on the banks of Rhine to the ground just because his horse got frightened by sound of cannon fire from within.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nSingle balled males due to lack of yin-yang can behave this way. Even poor Hitler had a one eyed willie-- damaged in first world war.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nNapoleon for all his bravery was terrified of cats.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE9JgVPQ5I/AAAAAAAAA9Y/X-NAKeHUs_k/s1600/imagesCAYJFHTK.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE9JgVPQ5I/AAAAAAAAA9Y/X-NAKeHUs_k/s1600/imagesCAYJFHTK.jpg\" style=\"cursor: move;\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nWhile at St Helena he was secretly ( open secret ) wooing the gorgeous young wife of Count Montholon. Her third girl child conceived on the island was named Napoleone.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nOn Napoleons death he had willed that she should get a lock of his hair. It is from Napoleons hair that it was revealed that he dies of Arsenic poisoning , with advance of science later. It is presumed that Count Montholon poisoned him in short frequent doses.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nUni-balled Napoleon and Hitler, as predicted by Nostradamus, came to power at the age of 44, both attacked Russia at the age of 52, and both lost the war at the age of 56. Both underestimated the ice of Russia.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-7I-V6Se-5yg/TWyGIqYiMvI/AAAAAAAADy8/FmuXaFi_Z08/s1600/napoleons_retreat_from_moscow.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"227\" src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/-7I-V6Se-5yg/TWyGIqYiMvI/AAAAAAAADy8/FmuXaFi_Z08/s320/napoleons_retreat_from_moscow.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE-B52aDeI/AAAAAAAAA9c/dK5FHoRvKfE/s1600/imagesCALWCZYM.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE-B52aDeI/AAAAAAAAA9c/dK5FHoRvKfE/s1600/imagesCALWCZYM.jpg\" style=\"cursor: move;\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nNapoleon annulled his marriage with Josephine because she could NOT conceive. Her daughter Hortense ( from Alexandre ) later became the queen of Holland. Jospehine was not infertile. She had fudged her marriage certificate to make her younger on paper. Her age and Napoleons single ball could not do the trick.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE5u-Kvx3I/AAAAAAAAA84/JxoR9cBcERE/s1600/imagesCAP164WJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE5u-Kvx3I/AAAAAAAAA84/JxoR9cBcERE/s1600/imagesCAP164WJ.jpg\" style=\"cursor: move;\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\nOn his wedding night her possesive dog --a pug-- Fortune bit Napoleon savagely on his leg. Josephine thought he was crying out of sheer pleasure initially.</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin: 0px; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPE6DwrztvI/AAAAAAAAA88/LQLuTiMJDkI/s1600/imagesCAWLKRA0.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; THE BOOKS IS STILL IN MY HOME LIBRARY..<br />\n<br />\nHIS QUATRAINS ARE VAGUE\u2026.<br />\n<br />\nPEOPLE LIKE HITLERs NAME WAS CONVERTED TO HISTER TO ACCOMODATE THE PREDICTIONS..<br />\n<br />\nJEW HITLER WAS USED BY ROTHSCHILD TO CARVE OUT ISRAEL -- HIS ORIGINAL NAME WAS NOT HILTER ( BUT HEIDLER AS PER SCHOOL RECORDS )-- IT WAS GRANTED TO HIM..<br />\n<br />\nTHIS IS A PERFECT CASE OF CREATING TRUTHS VIA THE BACK DOOR..<br />\n<br />\nDURING WW1 AND WW2 --ROTHSCHILD DROPPED LEAFLETS ALL OVER EUROPE QUOTING NOSTRADAMUS\u2026<br />\n<br />\nThe book of predictions is Les Propheties, a collection of 942 poetic quatrains allegedly predicting future events. The book was first published in 1555 and has rarely been out of print since his death. ..WHY ?..<br />\n<br />\nWHO IS SO KEEN ON PROPAGATING THE FAME AND POWERS ( SIC) OF NOSTRADAMUS ..</div>\n<div>\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">JEW NOSTRADAMUS WAS MADE POPULAR BY HIS ALMANAC WHICH WAS LIFTED FROM KERALA ..</span></span></div>\n<br />\nCapt Ajit Vadakayil declares today at 1105 AM, on 4th Jan 2018-- SATYA VACHAN that Nostradamus's predictions have been DELIBERATELY kept vague-- they could be applied to virtually anything, and are 100% useless for determining whether Nostradamus had any real prophetic powers. ..<br />\n<br />\nMost of the quatrains deal with disasters, such as plagues, earthquakes, wars, floods, invasions, murders, droughts, and battles\u2014all undated-..<br />\n<br />\nANY CHARLATAN CAN WRITE SUCH QUATRAINS \u2026<br />\n<br />\nOUR OWN VEDAS HAS SUCH COOKED UP VERSES INJECTED --BY JEW ROTHSCHILD..<br />\n<br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">THE FRENCH REVOLUTION WAS WORKED VIA BACKDOOR BY FRENCH ROTHSCHILDs FREEMASONS --THIS WAS THE FIRST REAL VICTORY OF FAKE NOSTRADAMUS..</span></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: 16px;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2015/11/the-french-revolution-conceived-and.html</span><br />\n<br />\nBELOW IS THE FRENCH REVOLUTION PREDICTION..( BULLSHIT )..<br />\n<br />\nTHE TRUTH IS ROTHSCHILDs MEDIA LIE THAT THEY HEARD THE QUEEN SAYING \"IF PEOPLE DONT HAVE BREAD LET THEM EAT CAKE \"..<br />\n<br />\nCentury VI.--Quatrain 74.<br />\n<br />\nLa. dechass\u00e9e 1 an regne tournera,<br />\nSes ennemies trouv\u00e9s des conjur\u00e9s:<br />\nPlus que jamais son temps triomphera,<br />\nTrois et septante \u00e0 mort trop asseur\u00e9s.<br />\n<br />\nTranslation.<br />\n<br />\nShe who was proscribed will return to the kingdom,<br />\nHer enemies will be treated as conspirators;<br />\nMore than ever her time (or empire) will triumph;<br />\nSeventy-three years its deathly domination is assured.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://www.sacred-texts.com/nos/oon/oon15.htm</span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\nHis astrologies were disastrously wrong, containing flagrant astronomical errors\u2014we in Kerala know astronomy..<br />\n<br />\nHe did not use a bowl of water as a \"magic mirror\" when writing his prophecies, he used a regular mirror. ..<br />\n<br />\nJEW ROTHSCHILD MATCHED HIS DEATH DATE ON LATER EDITIONS\u2026<br />\n<br />\nIf he predicted his own death in Presage 141, he missed it by a year \u2014 so some editions show a version of that Presage posthumously edited by his secretary to match the correct date\u2026<br />\n<br />\nNostradamus was reputed to be a plague doctor\u2014he knew SHIT about plague..<br />\n<br />\nJEW ROTHSCHILD GAVE BULL THAT NOSTRADAMUS WAS BURIED UPRIGHT LIKE HINDU JIVAN MUKTS .. IN REALITY HE WAS BURIED IN LYING POSITION<br />\n<br />\nThe RIDICULOUS tale about Nostradamus is that he was buried standing up so that nobody would step on his grave; and when his body was later disinterred during the French Revolution to be relocated, he was wearing a FORGED medallion on which the exact date of the disinterment was engraved\u2026<br />\n<br />\nI have two editions of his book Les Propheties\u2014both are different to accommodate LIES converted to truths ..<br />\n<br />\nVarious versions were published during his lifetime, and there is no one authoritative collection<br />\n<br />\nOver 200 different translations and interpreted versions have been published since his death, so the folly of hoping to find Nostradamus' original text is IMPOSSIBLE..<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 2-<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"comment-actions secondary-text\" id=\"bc_0_15MN\" kind=\"m\" style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" id=\"bc_0_15BR\" style=\"font-size: 16px; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "21", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/7821982866859609572/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "2439597816253860569", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-02-10T13:22:00+05:30", "updated": "2014-09-23T09:47:08+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNDExNDQ1ODI4NjQyCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/02/vipassana-meditation-capt-ajit.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/2439597816253860569", "title": "VIPASSANA MEDITATION-  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<iframe allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"344\" src=\"http://www.youtube.com/embed/h9OVvmZ8CZg?fs=1\" width=\"425\"></iframe><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">My son at Cornell ( doing his ME in computer science ) &nbsp;is playing a meditative piece done by Ludovico Einaudi, the Italian , whose grandfather was the President Of Italy from 1948-55.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\">I am writing about Vipassana meditation .</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3ErD3B1nEgQ/TVOYhqeDVII/AAAAAAAADUY/pJnvyC3N0Qc/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3ErD3B1nEgQ/TVOYhqeDVII/AAAAAAAADUY/pJnvyC3N0Qc/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" height=\"299\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Vipashayna is a Sanskrit word , and it is called Vipassana is Pali.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Vipashyana meditation was started on the banks of the river Sraswati by the vedic seers in 9000 BC. The Rig Veda written in 5000 BC talks about Vipashyana meditation.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">It was Buddha who re-discovered Vipassana . Buddha did not teach in Sanskrit, he taught in the local language . This is why more than 50% of the world hold him in great respect ( though Buddism is almost extinct in India , as Hindus believe in the immortality of DNA ).&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Buddha however was born as a Hindu, lived as a Hindu and died as a Hindu. 8 strands of his hair are preserved in Yangoon Burma inside the Shwedagon Pagode. This can be subjected to a DNA test to establish when he actually walked on this planet. Max Mueller had declared that he was born in 563 BC , to please the Vatican. If Vatican had their way they would have put it in AD.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Now getting back to the piano score-- Meditation is an exercise of the mind. What physical exercise is to the body, meditation is to the mind. Silencing the body is easy, but silencing the mind is difficult in this modern age. Silencing is about grace, harmony and tranquility. Exhaustion is NOT tranquility.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">In the modern age people get stressed, and they need to still the mind--the chattering monkey, which remains entangled in the past and the imagined future, but never in the present.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">Vipassana meditation is about holding your mind to the present.</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\"></span> It is the search for inner strength. It is NOT a drill. It has to be done with grace. Your mind cant keep going round and round in circles, etching a deep groove and make the subject deep rooted. Beware of the spiritually arrogant, such persons cant be proper Gurus.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">A person stops thinking either when he is dead or when he has realised. When your ego powered mind is chattering like a monkey or the angry sea, you miss the truth. Truth can be communicated only in silence. For this deep silence you need to have harmony between the mind, body and soul.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The aim of every form of meditation is to still the mind, or you cant purify it and get rid of deep rooted negativities , which affect your health and even give you severe migraines.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red;\">Vipassana is a surgical operation of your subconscious mind to remove and discard negativity / ego and improve tolerance, grace and kindness.</span>&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">An ideal candidate would be Donald Trump.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Vipassana uses the awareness of breath method. The meditator sees the cosmos as nothing but the tiniest packet of quantum energy. It makes you a watcher and a witness. Such a person cannot be an egoist. The art of observing is to help you feel separate from all that you are clinging to.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">For a layman-- you are stressed when your hands feel cold, your heart rate, breathing, and muscle tension increases. The result is that your immune system goes for a toss and you get depressed or burnt out.. Depression is a weird feeling of loss .</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Vipassana teaches you to look inwards, with awareness , withing yourself and know the true nature of all sensations, and loosen the stranglehold of habits and vices.. he scans his own body and sees where the stress and tension is.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">He just witnesses , he does not react. His mind does not control him, rather he controls his mind.</span> It is a universal remedy for all universal ills.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Find a quiet place to sit for 15 minutes. place where you can sit comfortably, undisturbed, for at least 20 minutes. Background noises like the sound of a car horn or a ticking clock should not be considered hindrances, and in fact can be legitimate objects of mindfulness. Don't wear earplugs .&nbsp;&nbsp;Wear loose clothing &nbsp;and be bare feet. Sit with your&nbsp;back and head held straight. You may sit on the floor or in a chair. Keep your eyes closed. If you must move, notice how and why you are moving.<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Simply be mindful of in-and-out breathing. </span>You may feel that your breathing is too short, too long, too gentle or too heavy. Do not try to control it. Stop judging. Just let it be, let it settle by itself as you watch.<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;It is the process of watching which is the meditation, not what you are watching.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When you become distracted, gently refocus your attention on your breathing. Keep watching. Just breathe... As the abdomen rises, observe the motion from beginning to end with your mind. When the abdomen falls, do the same. That's it. Just keep watching the rising-falling movements. You don't have to do anything to them. Just know the movements without judging or describing them.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Restrict your attention to what is occurring in the&nbsp;<i>immediate present moment</i>. Don't think about the past or future\u2014 don't think about anything at all. Let go of worries, concerns, and memories. Empty your mind of everything except the movements occurring right now. But don't&nbsp;<i>think</i>&nbsp;about the motions; just&nbsp;<i>know</i>&nbsp;them.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"background-color: white;\">In insight meditation the aim is not to think, but only to know</span>.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">As the abdomen expands, say the word \"rising\" in your mind. When it contracts, say \"falling.\" Continue to note rising, falling, rising, falling, from one moment to the next.</span>&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-FTGBFWCs9sg/TVOY4x_4NqI/AAAAAAAADUc/zIFlxcUIuc4/s1600/a.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-FTGBFWCs9sg/TVOY4x_4NqI/AAAAAAAADUc/zIFlxcUIuc4/s320/a.gif\" height=\"200\" width=\"320\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Ninety-percent of your attention should be on the actual movement instead of on the label. The aim in Vipassana is to know the object itself, not the word.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The abdomen should not be visualized. You only have to know the movements. Be sure to breathe naturally; don't try to control the breath in any way. A mental note identifies the object in general but not in detail. For example, when a sound pulls your attention away, label it \"hearing\" instead of car horn,\" \"voices\" or \"barking dog.\"&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If an unpleasant sensation arises, note \"pain \" or \"feeling\" instead of \"knee pain\" or \"my back pain.\" Then return your attention to the primary object. When aware of a fragrance, say the mental note \"smelling\" for a moment or two. You don't have to identify the scent.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">The motto is: \"Focus and forget it,\" or \"know and let go.\"</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Healing is NOT a physical process, rather it is mental. Mind can wipe mistakes off the DNA blueprint and destroy any disease that has disturbed the design. DNA's ability to repair itself is affected adversely when a person is in depression. Meditation experiences silence, and is devoid of drives, wishes, fears , thoughts and emotions. Afterwards when the mind returns to its usual level of consciousness, it has acquired some freedom to move..&nbsp; </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-zLxiOZwpkDo/TVOYb2hp9kI/AAAAAAAADUU/IdasV5-C0LA/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-zLxiOZwpkDo/TVOYb2hp9kI/AAAAAAAADUU/IdasV5-C0LA/s1600/images.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 9pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: normal;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Grace and peace are the hallmarks of a healthy non-delusional mind in a healthy body.. The happiness is stable.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: normal;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-hcsaaZnfa5A/TVOYXfMSxcI/AAAAAAAADUQ/oWDAsAPsiGw/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-hcsaaZnfa5A/TVOYXfMSxcI/AAAAAAAADUQ/oWDAsAPsiGw/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Gurus of Vipassana meditation do not charge fees, unlike Reiki masters, who must charge as a rule.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">People bought stock on margin or credit for as little as 10% down. They then used the stock as collateral to borrow more money to buy more stock. Then they did it again. The market was a free-for-all. It was prosperity heaven.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; This meant that both stockbrokers and customers had to dump their stocks on the market to cover their loans, no matter what price they had to sell them for. As a result, the market tumbled and that day was known as \"Black Thursday\".<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Curtis Dall, a broker for Lehman brothers, was on the floor of the NY stock exchange the day of the crash. Model T became so famous, people considered it a norm. More than 15 million Model Ts were manufactured in all, reaching a rate of more than 10,000 cars a day in 1925, or 2 million annually..</span><br />\n<br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\">The Model T and Volkswagen are similar cars because the Germans Jew workers stole the Ford design and sent it to Germany. .</span></div>\n<br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\">Volkswagen was automaker founded on 28 May 1937 by the German Labour Front under JEW Adolf Hitler and headquartered in Wolfsburg. Rothschild was a sleeping partner with major stake in the car factory.</span><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"></span><br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">To sell his Volkswagen cars Rothschild needed to STOP the export of Ford cars to Europe. Pretty soon Volkswagen knocked of Ford\u2019s Model T as the No 1 selling car.</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">MY REVELATIOS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;</span><span style=\"color: red; Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/05/hum-honge-kaamyaab-capt-ajit-vadakayil.html?showComment=1525367274643#c2514935488816632213\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">May 3, 2018 at 10:37 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_190MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/05/hum-honge-kaamyaab-capt-ajit-vadakayil.html</span><br /><br />The International Jew is a four-volume set of books which exposed Rothschild and his Jews.. It was distributed in the early 1920s by Henry Ford.<br /><br /><span style=\"color: red;\">https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_International_Jew</span><br /><br />The Dearborn Independent, also known as The Ford International Weekly, was a weekly newspaper established in 1901, and published by Henry Ford from 1919 through 1927. The paper reached a circulation of 900,000 by 1925, second only to the New York Daily News run from the shadows by Jew Rothschild.<br /><br />Henry Ford knew that Jew Rothschild would start world wars to carve out the state of Israel and to make money out of war. Ford wrote that parasite Jews, in their role as financiers, contributed nothing of value to society.<br /><br />Ford once bit into a candy bar and, finding it not as good as it once had been, said \"The Jews have taken hold of it. They've cheapened it to make more money\".<br /><br />In 1915 Ford blamed Jews for instigating World War I, saying \"I know who caused the war: German-Jewish bankers.\"<br /><br />In 1925, Ford said \"What I oppose most is the international Jewish money power that is met in every war. That is what I oppose \u2013 a power that has no country and that can order the young men of all countries out to death.\"<br /><br />One of the articles, \"Jewish Power and America's Money Famine\", asserted that the power exercised by Jews over the nation's supply of money was insidious, depriving farmers and others outside the banking coterie of money when they needed it most. The article asked the question: \"Where is the American gold supply? ... It may be in the United States but it does not belong to the United States.\" It concluded that Jews controlled the gold supply and, hence, American money<br />Another article, \"Jewish Idea Molded Federal Reserve System\", was a reflection of Ford's distrust of the Federal Reserve System and its proponent, Paul Warburg. Ford believed the Federal Reserve system was secretive and insidious<br /><br />Many issues of the Independent comment extensively upon The Protocols of the Elders of Zion. The first mention of the Protocols appears in the issue of July 10, 1920, the seventh installment of its \"International Jew\" series.<br /><br />Also, in 1920\u201321 the Independent carried a series of articles expanding on the themes of financial control by Jews, entitled:-----<br /><br />Jewish Idea in American Monetary Affairs: The remarkable story of Paul Warburg, who began work on the United States monetary system after three weeks residence in this country<br />Jewish Idea Molded Federal Reserve System: What Baruch was in War Material, Paul Warburg was in War Finances; Some Curious revelations of money and politics.<br />Jewish Idea of a Central Bank for America: The evolution of Paul M. Warburg's idea of Federal Reserve System without government management.<br />How Jewish International Finance Functions: The Warburg family and firm divided the world between them and did amazing things which non-Jews could not do<br />Jewish Power and America's Money Famine: The Warburg Federal Reserve sucks money to New York, leaving productive sections of the country in disastrous need.<br />The Economic Plan of International Jews: An outline of the Protocolists' monetary policy, with notes on the parallel found in Jewish financial practice.<br /><br /><span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/01/murky-truths-of-inflation-and.html<br /><br />http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/02/worth-more-than-sum-total-of-entire.html</span><br /><br />The ADL mobilized prominent Jews to publicly oppose Ford's message. They formed a coalition of Jewish groups for the same purpose and raised constant objections in the Detroit press. Before leaving his presidency early in 1921, Rothschild\u2019s agent Woodrow Wilson joined other leading Americans in a statement that rebuked Ford and others for their antisemitic campaign<br /><br />Capt ajit vadakayil<br />..</div>\n</div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_174B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"background-color: #eeeeee;
